<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">Because of You (Kelly Clarkson song)</h1>
<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
<div id="contentSub"></div>
<div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">

<p>"<b>Because of You</b>" is a song recorded by American pop singer <a href="/wiki/Kelly_Clarkson" title="Kelly Clarkson">Kelly Clarkson</a> for her second studio album, <i><a href="/wiki/Breakaway_(Kelly_Clarkson_album)" title="Breakaway (Kelly Clarkson album)">Breakaway</a></i> (2004). It was written by Clarkson along with its producers <a href="/wiki/David_Hodges" title="David Hodges">David Hodges</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ben_Moody" title="Ben Moody">Ben Moody</a>. It was released on August 16, 2005 by <a href="/wiki/RCA_Records" title="RCA Records">RCA Records</a>, as the third single from <i>Breakaway</i>. Clarkson originally wrote "Because of You" when she was 16 years old to cope with the emotional distress caused by her parents' divorce. She wanted the song to be included on her debut studio album, <i><a href="/wiki/Thankful_(Kelly_Clarkson_album)" title="Thankful (Kelly Clarkson album)">Thankful</a></i> (2003), but her record label rejected the song. She then polished the song with Hodges and Moody before successfully convincing her label to include it on <i>Breakaway</i>.</p>
<p>Lyrically, "Because of You" explores the pain of a deteriorating relationship with her father. Critics noted that the lyrics are Clarkson's ode to her father. The song begins with a piano-led melody and as it launches into the chorus, the sound of a roaring guitar becomes apparent. "Because of You" received positive reviews from music critics, who complimented its expressive lyrics, creative arrangement and Clarkson's vocal prowess. It peaked at number seven on the <a href="/wiki/Billboard_Hot_100" title="Billboard Hot 100"><i>Billboard</i> Hot 100</a> and sold over 1.5 million digital downloads in the United States. It was certified platinum by the <a href="/wiki/Recording_Industry_Association_of_America" title="Recording Industry Association of America">Recording Industry Association of America</a> (RIAA). "Because of You" became Clarkson's biggest success in Europe, topping the <a href="/wiki/European_Hot_100_Singles" title="European Hot 100 Singles">European Hot 100 Singles</a> chart. It also reached number one in the Netherlands, Denmark and Switzerland, as well as the top ten in Australia, Austria, Canada, Germany, Belgium, Hungary, Ireland, and the United Kingdom.</p>
<p>The song's accompanying music video was directed by <a href="/wiki/Vadim_Perelman" title="Vadim Perelman">Vadim Perelman</a>. Clarkson wrote the treatment for the video herself in order to reflect the pain that she felt due to her parents' divorce. The video's plot centers on Clarkson engaging in a heated argument with her husband in front of her child before realizing that she was repeating her parents' mistake. It won in the category for <a href="/wiki/MTV_Video_Music_Award_for_Best_Female_Video" title="MTV Video Music Award for Best Female Video">Best Female Video</a> at the 2006 MTV Video Music Awards. "Because of You" was performed live at numerous venues, including the <a href="/wiki/My_December_Tour" title="My December Tour">My December Tour</a> (2007) as well as the <a href="/wiki/All_I_Ever_Wanted_Tour" title="All I Ever Wanted Tour">All I Ever Wanted Tour</a> (2009). It was covered by several artists including <a href="/wiki/Ronan_Parke" title="Ronan Parke">Ronan Parke</a>, who was a runner-up in the <a href="/wiki/Britain%27s_Got_Talent_(series_5)" title="Britain's Got Talent (series 5)">fifth series</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Britain%27s_Got_Talent" title="Britain's Got Talent">Britain's Got Talent</a></i>, and added to the international soundtrack of Brazilian <a href="/wiki/Soap_opera" title="Soap opera">soap opera</a> <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bel%C3%ADssima" title="Belíssima">Belíssima</a></i>. In 2007, the song was recorded by <a href="/wiki/Reba_McEntire" title="Reba McEntire">Reba McEntire</a> as a duet with Clarkson, which was released as a lead single for McEntire's twenty-fourth studio album <i><a href="/wiki/Reba:_Duets" title="Reba: Duets">Reba: Duets</a></i>. "<a href="/wiki/Piece_by_Piece_(Kelly_Clarkson_song)" title="Piece by Piece (Kelly Clarkson song)">Piece by Piece</a>", the title track from Clarkson's <a href="/wiki/Piece_by_Piece_(Kelly_Clarkson_album)" title="Piece by Piece (Kelly Clarkson album)">seventh studio album</a>, serves as the canonical sequel to "Because of You".</p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Background_and_writing">Background and writing</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Because_of_You_(Kelly_Clarkson_song)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Background and writing">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quotebox" style="float: left; clear: left; margin: 0.5em 1.4em 0.8em 0; width:25%; padding: 6px; border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 88%; background-color: #F9F9F9;">
<div class="" style="position: relative; text-align: left;">
<div>
<p>"My biggest song worldwide is Because of You, and … you may as well grab a knife. That song really is the most depressing one I've ever written. I tried to get it on <i>Thankful</i>, and was laughed at and told I wasn't a good writer. So then I tried to get it on <i>Breakaway</i> – and the label saw the results, people responding to it, and allowed it to become a single. Then took credit for its success, of course."</p>
</div>
</div>
<cite style="display: block; text-align: left;">—Clarkson on trying to get the track into her album, <i>Thankful</i>.</cite>
<p><cite style="display: block; text-align: left;"><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-guardian_1-0"><a href="#cite_note-guardian-1">[1]</a></sup></cite></p>
</div>
<p>"Because of You" was written by Clarkson alongside its producer, David Hodges and Ben Moody.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MTV_2-0"><a href="#cite_note-MTV-2">[2]</a></sup> They also wrote and produced another track, titled "Addicted", that appeared in Clarkson's album <i><a href="/wiki/Breakaway_(Kelly_Clarkson_album)" title="Breakaway (Kelly Clarkson album)">Breakaway</a></i> (2004).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MTV_News_3-0"><a href="#cite_note-MTV_News-3">[3]</a></sup> Clarkson originally wrote "Because of You" when she was 16 years old as a means of coping with the emotional distress caused by the divorce of her parents.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup> She wrote the lyrics of the song in less than 25 minutes.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-autogenerated1_5-0"><a href="#cite_note-autogenerated1-5">[5]</a></sup></p>
<p>In an interview with <i><a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">The Guardian</a></i>, Clarkson said that she wanted to include the song in her first album, <i><a href="/wiki/Thankful_(Kelly_Clarkson_album)" title="Thankful (Kelly Clarkson album)">Thankful</a></i> (2003), but she was laughed at.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-guardian_1-1"><a href="#cite_note-guardian-1">[1]</a></sup> Then, she took the initiative to polish the song by sending a tape to Moody and Hodges, whom later worked with her and received co-writing credit of the song. Clarkson explained, "Hearing the Evanescence album, you can obviously tell that David and Ben have a real passion for music and that big kind of background. And I have a big voice and I like the music to match it, so it was a real dream team."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MTV_News_3-1"><a href="#cite_note-MTV_News-3">[3]</a></sup></p>
<p>According to Moody, he was very impressed with Clarkson and the song itself, saying "She had these ideas already in place for songs; all I really had to do was build music around them and develop them. It was quite easy."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MTV_2-1"><a href="#cite_note-MTV-2">[2]</a></sup> Clarkson also admitted that "Because of You" is the most depressing song she has ever written.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-guardian_1-2"><a href="#cite_note-guardian-1">[1]</a></sup> Despite the revelation, she told <i><a href="/wiki/Entertainment_Weekly" title="Entertainment Weekly">Entertainment Weekly</a></i> in August 2011 that she wanted to be remembered for the song because she had to work hard to get it on <i>Breakaway</i> (2004) when everyone was against it. She added, "I think I’m most proud of that song – just getting it on an album because no one liked it until it hit no. 1 worldwide and everybody was on board."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Composition">Composition</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Because_of_You_(Kelly_Clarkson_song)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Composition">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="mbox-small" role="presentation" style="border:1px solid #aaa;background-color:#f9f9f9;">
<tr>
<td class="mbox-image">
<div class="center">
<div class="floatnone"><img alt="" data-file-height="160" data-file-width="160" height="50" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Gnome-mime-sound-openclipart.svg/50px-Gnome-mime-sound-openclipart.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Gnome-mime-sound-openclipart.svg/75px-Gnome-mime-sound-openclipart.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Gnome-mime-sound-openclipart.svg/100px-Gnome-mime-sound-openclipart.svg.png 2x" width="50"/></div>
</div>
</td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist" style="line-height:1.1em">
<div class="haudio">
<div style="padding:4px 0"><a href="/wiki/File:Kelly_Clarkson_-_Because_Of_You.ogg" title="File:Kelly Clarkson - Because Of You.ogg">"Because of You" (2004)</a></div>
<div>
<div class="mediaContainer" style="width:220px"><audio class="kskin" controls="" data-durationhint="20.845714285714" data-mwprovider="local" data-mwtitle="Kelly_Clarkson_-_Because_Of_You.ogg" data-startoffset="0" id="mwe_player_0" preload="none" style="width:220px">
<source data-bandwidth="51177" data-height="0" data-shorttitle="Ogg source" data-title="Original Ogg file (51 kbps)" data-width="0" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/7/71/Kelly_Clarkson_-_Because_Of_You.ogg" type='audio/ogg; codecs="vorbis"'></source></audio></div>
</div>
<div class="description" style="padding:2px 0 0 0">"Because of You" is a piano ballad composed in F minor.</div>
</div>
<hr/></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="mbox-text" colspan="2" style="line-height:1.1em"><span><i>Problems playing this file? See <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Media_help" title="Wikipedia:Media help">media help</a>.</i></span></td>
</tr>
</table>
<p>"Because of You" is a piano ballad<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup> with a length of three minutes and 39 seconds.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup> It is set in <a href="/wiki/Time_signature" title="Time signature">common time</a> and has a moderate <a href="/wiki/Tempo" title="Tempo">tempo</a> of 69 beats per minute. It is composed in the key of <a href="/wiki/F_minor" title="F minor">F minor</a>, and then modulated to the key of <a href="/wiki/G_minor" title="G minor">G minor</a>, with Clarkson's vocal range spanning over two octaves from A<sub>b3</sub> to E<sub>b5</sub>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup> Tony Heywood of <a href="/wiki/MusicOMH" title="MusicOMH">MusicOMH</a> noted that the song's piano arrangement is reminiscent of <a href="/wiki/Tori_Amos" title="Tori Amos">Tori Amos</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-musicomh_10-0"><a href="#cite_note-musicomh-10">[10]</a></sup> Lyrically, "Because of You" is a fiery ode to Clarkson's father,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Sput_11-0"><a href="#cite_note-Sput-11">[11]</a></sup> and begins with Clarkson singing "oohs" over a somber piano which creates a "wintry tone."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup> As the song launches into the chorus, the roaring guitar is evident,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup> and the lyrics, "Because of you I never stray too far from the sidewalk / Because of you I learned to play on the safe side so I don’t get hurt," were deemed as "touching" by Dave Donelly of <a href="/wiki/Sputnikmusic" title="Sputnikmusic">Sputnikmusic</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Sput_11-1"><a href="#cite_note-Sput-11">[11]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Critical_reception">Critical reception</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Because_of_You_(Kelly_Clarkson_song)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Critical reception">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>"Because of You" received universal critical acclaim. Film Laureate of Blogcritics considered "Because of You" and "Where Is Your Heart" as his two favorite songs from <i>Breakaway,</i> writing "[Clarkson] commands these two songs like a seasoned pro and directs herself in her songs the way Steven Spielberg said Barbra Streisand directs herself in her songs as if she's directing an actor in a movie."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup> Dave Donnelly of <a href="/wiki/Sputnikmusic" title="Sputnikmusic">Sputnikmusic</a> compared the song to <a href="/wiki/Evanescence" title="Evanescence">Evanescence</a>'s "<a href="/wiki/My_Immortal" title="My Immortal">My Immortal</a>" (2003). (Note that two of the songwriters and producers of "My Immortal" were also involved in this track.) He added that Clarkson managed to take the piano-driven song in a different direction with a "stormy, hard blues vocal... avoiding the typical raised-key final chorus cliché along the way".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Sput_11-2"><a href="#cite_note-Sput-11">[11]</a></sup> Christa L. Titus of <i><a href="/wiki/Billboard_(magazine)" title="Billboard (magazine)">Billboard</a></i> lauded the song for its absence of schmaltz factor, "only a potent, pained, grown-up anthem of gross betrayal and loss." She concluded her review, writing "it is time for Clarkson to return to No. 1 on the <a href="/wiki/Billboard_Hot_100" title="Billboard Hot 100"><i>Billboard</i> Hot 100</a>; she has certainly become the most consistent hope for top 40 staple status."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup> Critics also lauded Clarkson's vocal prowess in the song. Pam Avoledo of Blogcritics thought that vocally, the song is Clarkson's "shining" moment.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup> Tony Heywood of MusicOMH noted that in the song, Clarkson's voice is "full of vulnerability, ache and wounded pride."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-musicomh_10-1"><a href="#cite_note-musicomh-10">[10]</a></sup> In May 15, 2007, the song was listed as one of the recipients of BMI Pop Awards.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup> At the 24th ASCAP Pop Music Awards, the song was honoured with the Most Performed Songs award.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup> On July 2008, <a href="/wiki/BBC_News" title="BBC News">BBC News</a> reported that according to <a href="/wiki/PRS_for_Music" title="PRS for Music">Performing Right Society</a>, "Because of You" was the second most played song in the United Kingdom over the last five years, following <a href="/wiki/Daniel_Powter" title="Daniel Powter">Daniel Powter</a>'s "<a href="/wiki/Bad_Day_(Daniel_Powter_song)" title="Bad Day (Daniel Powter song)">Bad Day</a>" (2005).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup> On March 5, 2013, <i><a href="/wiki/Billboard_(magazine)" title="Billboard (magazine)">Billboard</a></i>, ranked the song #7 in its list of Top 100 American Idol Hits of All Time.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Commercial_performance">Commercial performance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Because_of_You_(Kelly_Clarkson_song)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Commercial performance">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>"Because of You" entered the <a href="/wiki/Billboard_Hot_100" title="Billboard Hot 100"><i>Billboard</i> Hot 100</a> at number 99 on the week ending September 3, 2005.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21"><a href="#cite_note-21">[21]</a></sup> On November 19, 2005, the song peaked at number seven and became her sixth single to reach the top-ten.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22"><a href="#cite_note-22">[22]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23"><a href="#cite_note-23">[23]</a></sup> It also topped the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mainstream_Top_40_(Pop_Songs)" title="Mainstream Top 40 (Pop Songs)">Pop Songs</a> chart on the week ending October 29, 2005.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24"><a href="#cite_note-24">[24]</a></sup> It became the seventh best selling single of the 2000s decade on the Pop Songs chart complied by <i>Billboard</i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25"><a href="#cite_note-25">[25]</a></sup> On January 31, 2008, "Because of You" was certified <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/RIAA_certifications" title="RIAA certifications">platinum</a> by the <a href="/wiki/Recording_Industry_Association_of_America" title="Recording Industry Association of America">Recording Industry Association of America</a> (RIAA).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-platinum_riaa_26-0"><a href="#cite_note-platinum_riaa-26">[26]</a></sup> As of March 2013, the song has sold 1,803,000 digital copies in the United States.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup> In Canada, "Because of You" debuted at number 60 on the <a href="/wiki/Canadian_Hot_100" title="Canadian Hot 100">Canadian Hot 100</a> on the week ending July 14, 2007.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28"><a href="#cite_note-28">[28]</a></sup> Two weeks later, the song jumped to a new peak at number 36 and stayed in the position for two weeks.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29"><a href="#cite_note-29">[29]</a></sup> It was certified gold by <a href="/wiki/Music_Canada" title="Music Canada">Music Canada</a> on December 4, 2007 for shipments over 40,000 units.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-mc_30-0"><a href="#cite_note-mc-30">[30]</a></sup> The single also appeared and peaked on the <a href="/wiki/UK_Singles_Chart" title="UK Singles Chart">UK Singles Chart</a> at number seven on the week ending December 4, 2005.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31"><a href="#cite_note-31">[31]</a></sup> As of April 2016, the song sold over 430,000 copies in the United Kingdom. <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32"><a href="#cite_note-32">[32]</a></sup></p>
<p>In Australia, the song debuted and peaked at number four on the issue dated December 5, 2005.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33"><a href="#cite_note-33">[33]</a></sup> It was certified <a href="/wiki/List_of_music_recording_certifications" title="List of music recording certifications">gold</a> by the <a href="/wiki/Australian_Recording_Industry_Association" title="Australian Recording Industry Association">Australian Recording Industry Association</a> (ARIA) for shipments over 35,000 units.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-gold_aria_34-0"><a href="#cite_note-gold_aria-34">[34]</a></sup> The song became the 58th best-selling single in Australia in 2006.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35"><a href="#cite_note-35">[35]</a></sup> In New Zealand, "Because of You" debuted on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_Zealand_Singles_Chart" title="New Zealand Singles Chart">New Zealand Singles Chart</a> at number 37 on the week ending December 5, 2005,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-36"><a href="#cite_note-36">[36]</a></sup> and peaked at number 19 two weeks later.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37"><a href="#cite_note-37">[37]</a></sup> On the week ending March 20, 2006, "Because of You" debuted at number eight on the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Media_Control_Charts" title="Media Control Charts">German Singles Chart</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-German_38-0"><a href="#cite_note-German-38">[38]</a></sup> Three weeks later, it peaked at number four and stayed in the position for three consecutive weeks.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-German_38-1"><a href="#cite_note-German-38">[38]</a></sup> The song was certified gold by <a href="/wiki/Bundesverband_Musikindustrie" title="Bundesverband Musikindustrie">The Federal Association of Music Industry</a> for shipments over 150,000 copies.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-gold_german_39-0"><a href="#cite_note-gold_german-39">[39]</a></sup> In Europe, "Because of You" received a commercial success. The song topped the charts in the Netherlands<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-40"><a href="#cite_note-40">[40]</a></sup> and Switzerland,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41"><a href="#cite_note-41">[41]</a></sup> and reached the top five in Austria,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42"><a href="#cite_note-42">[42]</a></sup> Belgium (Flanders),<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43"><a href="#cite_note-43">[43]</a></sup> Ireland<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-44"><a href="#cite_note-44">[44]</a></sup> and Norway.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-45"><a href="#cite_note-45">[45]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Music_video">Music video</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Because_of_You_(Kelly_Clarkson_song)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Music video">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Development">Development</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Because_of_You_(Kelly_Clarkson_song)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Development">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The accompanying <a href="/wiki/Music_video" title="Music video">music video</a> for "Because of You" was directed by <a href="/wiki/Vadim_Perelman" title="Vadim Perelman">Vadim Perelman</a> and was produced by Rhonda Vernet.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-46"><a href="#cite_note-46">[46]</a></sup> Clarkson wrote the treatment for the video herself in order to reflect the pain that she felt due to her parents' divorce.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-47"><a href="#cite_note-47">[47]</a></sup> Nevertheless, Clarkson also allowed Perelman to take control of the production of the video.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-video_48-0"><a href="#cite_note-video-48">[48]</a></sup> According to Perelman, he wanted to create a disconnection to show "that this kind of dysfunctional family can exist anywhere."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-premiere_49-0"><a href="#cite_note-premiere-49">[49]</a></sup> In an interview with MTV News, Clarkson confessed that the video is sad, rationalizing, "It's a sad song, so the video obviously has to follow that. But it ends really happy and everything and the family, my family, ends up breaking the cycle of my parents."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-video_48-1"><a href="#cite_note-video-48">[48]</a></sup> Since the music video deals specifically with her parents' divorce, Clarkson had to seek for her parents' permission. She explained,</p>
<blockquote>
<p>"It's very close to home [for me]. I OK'd it with my family and everything because they think it's important, because we're obviously very different now than we were when we were younger. And it's important for people to see that raw kind of emotion that happens in life. It sucks sometimes, so it's important to see that I think. And that's what we're portraying in the video."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-video_48-2"><a href="#cite_note-video-48">[48]</a></sup></p>
</blockquote>
<p>In the video, the younger version of Clarkson is played by Kennedy Nöel, the daughter of her musical director, Jason Halbert.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-50"><a href="#cite_note-50">[50]</a></sup> The video premiered on October 3, 2005, on <i><a href="/wiki/Total_Request_Live" title="Total Request Live">Total Request Live</a></i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-premiere_49-1"><a href="#cite_note-premiere-49">[49]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Synopsis">Synopsis</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Because_of_You_(Kelly_Clarkson_song)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Synopsis">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:232px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Kellyclarksonbecauseofyouvideo.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="220" data-file-width="400" height="127" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/5/56/Kellyclarksonbecauseofyouvideo.png/230px-Kellyclarksonbecauseofyouvideo.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/5/56/Kellyclarksonbecauseofyouvideo.png/345px-Kellyclarksonbecauseofyouvideo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/5/56/Kellyclarksonbecauseofyouvideo.png 2x" width="230"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Kellyclarksonbecauseofyouvideo.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Clarkson and her younger self (Kennedy Nöel) in the music video of "Because of You."</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The video starts at the Clarksons' household. There, she and her husband are engaged in a heated argument and he threatens to smash down a picture of the family at one point. Time freezes still and her husband becomes immobile; Clarkson, however, is immune to this. Looking around her house, she sees her younger self. Hand in hand, the younger and older versions of Clarkson relive her troubled childhood as various painful memories are seen, such as the younger Clarkson making a picture for her father who tosses it into the sink while talking on the phone, and Clarkson's mother making an unappreciated dinner for her father as she puts the father's dinner into the bin. These events drive her mother to the point of taking pills before closing the door in the younger Clarkson's face, so that she doesn't see her starting to cry. The breaking point is finally seen when Clarkson's parents have a physical fight and throw objects at each other. Soon after, Clarkson's father packs his bags and leaves despite the younger Clarkson's pleas for him to stay. The older Clarkson runs back in time to the present, and instead of fighting with her husband, they make up. They then see that their daughter in the video had seen them fight, and they embrace her and each other. Throughout the music video, Clarkson is shown singing on the front porch, her mother's bed and a room full of mirrors, reflecting an image of her younger self.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-video_48-3"><a href="#cite_note-video-48">[48]</a></sup> Note that Kelly is holding Kennedy's hand in the scene where the childhood memories are revealed.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Reception_and_accolades">Reception and accolades</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Because_of_You_(Kelly_Clarkson_song)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Reception and accolades">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Elizabeth Black of <a href="/wiki/VH1" title="VH1">VH1</a> ranked the music video at number four in her list of "Five Emotive Music Video Performances." She reasoned, "Kelly Clarkson practically sobs her way through this hurt and angry expression of the pain that the narrator’s father has caused her through his absence and lack of love."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-51"><a href="#cite_note-51">[51]</a></sup> The music video won the category of <a href="/wiki/MTV_Video_Music_Award_for_Best_Female_Video" title="MTV Video Music Award for Best Female Video">Best Female Video</a> at the <a href="/wiki/2006_MTV_Video_Music_Awards" title="2006 MTV Video Music Awards">2006 MTV Video Music Awards</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-52"><a href="#cite_note-52">[52]</a></sup> This marks the second time Clarkson has won the same category two years in a row; her first win in the category was at the <a href="/wiki/2005_MTV_Video_Music_Awards" title="2005 MTV Video Music Awards">2005 MTV Video Music Awards</a> for the music video of "<a href="/wiki/Since_U_Been_Gone" title="Since U Been Gone">Since U Been Gone</a>."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-53"><a href="#cite_note-53">[53]</a></sup> The music video was also nominated in the category of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/MTV_Video_Music_Award_-_Viewer%27s_Choice" title="MTV Video Music Award - Viewer's Choice">Viewer's Choice Award</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-54"><a href="#cite_note-54">[54]</a></sup> but lost to <a href="/wiki/Fall_Out_Boy" title="Fall Out Boy">Fall Out Boy</a>'s "<a href="/wiki/Dance,_Dance_(Fall_Out_Boy_song)" title="Dance, Dance (Fall Out Boy song)">Dance, Dance</a>" (2005).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-55"><a href="#cite_note-55">[55]</a></sup> At the <a href="/wiki/2006_MuchMusic_Video_Awards" title="2006 MuchMusic Video Awards">2006 MuchMusic Video Awards</a>, the music video won the category of <a href="/wiki/2006_MuchMusic_Video_Awards#People.27s_Choice:_Favourite_International_Artist" title="2006 MuchMusic Video Awards">People's Choice: Favourite International Artist</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-56"><a href="#cite_note-56">[56]</a></sup> The video was also nominated at the <a href="/wiki/MTV_Australia_Video_Music_Awards_2006" title="MTV Australia Video Music Awards 2006">2006 MTV Australia Video Music Awards</a> in the category of <a href="/wiki/MTV_Australia_Video_Music_Awards_2006#Best_Pop_Video" title="MTV Australia Video Music Awards 2006">Best Pop Video</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-57"><a href="#cite_note-57">[57]</a></sup> but lost to <a href="/wiki/Ashlee_Simpson" title="Ashlee Simpson">Ashlee Simpson</a>'s "<a href="/wiki/Boyfriend_(Ashlee_Simpson_song)" title="Boyfriend (Ashlee Simpson song)">Boyfriend</a>" (2005).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-58"><a href="#cite_note-58">[58]</a></sup> According to Jocelyn Vena of MTV, the video for "Because of You" was referenced in <a href="/wiki/Taylor_Swift" title="Taylor Swift">Taylor Swift</a>'s music video for "<a href="/wiki/Mine_(Taylor_Swift_song)" title="Mine (Taylor Swift song)">Mine</a>" (2010), writing "When Swift's character remembers the fights her parents used to have, her memories mirror Clarkson's attempts to exorcise the demons of her past to find love in her future."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-59"><a href="#cite_note-59">[59]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Live_performances">Live performances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Because_of_You_(Kelly_Clarkson_song)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Live performances">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Clarkson performed "Because of You" at the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/48th_Grammy_Awards" title="48th Grammy Awards">48th Grammy Awards</a> which took place on February 8, 2006, at the <a href="/wiki/Staples_Center" title="Staples Center">Staples Center</a> in <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles" title="Los Angeles">Los Angeles</a>, <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a>. Donning a red dress and singing from beside a grand piano, her performance in that event garnered positive reviews from critics. Elysa Gardner of <i><a href="/wiki/USA_Today" title="USA Today">USA Today</a></i> lauded Clarkson's performance and ranked it as one of the three best performances, writing, "The pre-performance clip of a girlish-looking Clarkson emphasized how little Kelly has matured. The girl most likely to escape the <i><a href="/wiki/American_Idol" title="American Idol">American Idol</a></i> stigma was in fine, creamy voice, and kept the Mariah-esque riffing to a minimum."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-60"><a href="#cite_note-60">[60]</a></sup> Robert Lloyd of <i><a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles_Times" title="Los Angeles Times">Los Angeles Times</a></i> considered Clarkson's performance as one of the highlights in the event and described her performance as a "thin-skinned rendition [...] in which her whole being seemed involved."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-61"><a href="#cite_note-61">[61]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Yahoo!_Music" title="Yahoo! Music">Yahoo! Music</a> praised Clarkson's rendition of the song, calling it "perfectly fine" despite the saying that it was "a little reminiscent of those many mediocre, superficial ballads trotted out on 'Idol.'"<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-62"><a href="#cite_note-62">[62]</a></sup> In 2016, the performance was listed by <i>Billboard</i> as one of Clarkson's ten "most powerful and undeniable performances."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-greatest_63-0"><a href="#cite_note-greatest-63">[63]</a></sup> Jason Scott of <i>Billboard</i> commented, "Here, Clarkson serves up her signature power ballad backed by lush orchestration, sending chills through the crowd shortly before picking up two statues: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Best_Pop_Vocal_Album" title="Best Pop Vocal Album">best pop vocal album</a> for <i>Breakaway</i> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Best_Female_Pop_Vocal_Performance" title="Best Female Pop Vocal Performance">best female pop vocal performance</a> for "Since U Been Gone."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-greatest_63-1"><a href="#cite_note-greatest-63">[63]</a></sup></p>
<p>On August 21, 2007, Clarkson performed "Because of You" and "<a href="/wiki/Never_Again_(Kelly_Clarkson_song)" title="Never Again (Kelly Clarkson song)">Never Again</a>" (2007) on the <a href="/wiki/Canadian_Idol_(season_5)" title="Canadian Idol (season 5)">fifth season</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Canadian_Idol" title="Canadian Idol">Canadian Idol</a></i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-64"><a href="#cite_note-64">[64]</a></sup> "Because of You" was performed at the <a href="/wiki/My_December_Tour" title="My December Tour">My December Tour</a> (2007). Clarkson's performance of the song was accompanied only by <a href="/wiki/Wurlitzer" title="Wurlitzer">Wurlitzer organ</a> that earned her a prolonged ovation when she sent her voice soaring into the rafters.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-65"><a href="#cite_note-65">[65]</a></sup> While touring at <a href="/wiki/Beacon_Theatre_(New_York_City)" title="Beacon Theatre (New York City)">Beacon Theatre</a>, <a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">New York City</a>, Clarkson performed the song using only one keyboard, which was deemed by Donna Freydkin of <i>USA Today</i> as the most memorable moment of the event.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-66"><a href="#cite_note-66">[66]</a></sup> She also performed the song using only a keyboard as an instrument during her tour at <a href="/wiki/Massey_Hall" title="Massey Hall">Massey Hall</a>, <a href="/wiki/Toronto" title="Toronto">Toronto</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-67"><a href="#cite_note-67">[67]</a></sup> "Because of You" was also performed at the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Kelly_Clarkson_concert_tours#All_I_Ever_Wanted_Tour" title="List of Kelly Clarkson concert tours">All I Ever Wanted Tour</a> (2009). Clarkson's performance of the song during the tour in the <a href="/wiki/Hammerstein_Ballroom" title="Hammerstein Ballroom">Hammerstein Ballroom</a>, New York City, was given a positive review by Jim Cantiello of MTV. He explained that Clarkson's powerful rendition "literally stopped the show [...] for almost 30 seconds because the audience erupted in such wild applause."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-68"><a href="#cite_note-68">[68]</a></sup> Caryn Ganz of <i><a href="/wiki/Rolling_Stone" title="Rolling Stone">Rolling Stone</a></i> noted that Clarkson sang the song to pay homage to <a href="/wiki/Reba_McEntire" title="Reba McEntire">Reba McEntire</a> who was in the audience.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-69"><a href="#cite_note-69">[69]</a></sup></p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Year-end_charts">Year-end charts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Because_of_You_(Kelly_Clarkson_song)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Year-end charts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Cover_versions">Cover versions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Because_of_You_(Kelly_Clarkson_song)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Cover versions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><a href="/wiki/Lisa_Tucker_(singer)" title="Lisa Tucker (singer)">Lisa Tucker</a> covered the song on the <a href="/wiki/American_Idol_(season_5)" title="American Idol (season 5)">fifth season</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/American_Idol" title="American Idol">American Idol</a></i> in 2006. However, her performance was met with negative reviews from the judges and she was consequently eliminated from the show.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-130"><a href="#cite_note-130">[130]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-131"><a href="#cite_note-131">[131]</a></sup> On June 4, 2011, <i><a href="/wiki/Britain%27s_Got_Talent" title="Britain's Got Talent">Britain's Got Talent</a></i> contestant, <a href="/wiki/Ronan_Parke" title="Ronan Parke">Ronan Parke</a> covered "Because of You" in the finale of the <a href="/wiki/Britain%27s_Got_Talent_(series_5)" title="Britain's Got Talent (series 5)">fifth series</a> of the show. His performance garnered standing ovation from the audience as well as the four judges.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-132"><a href="#cite_note-132">[132]</a></sup> Parke also recorded the song and included it in his debut album, <i><a href="/wiki/Ronan_Parke_(album)" title="Ronan Parke (album)">Ronan Parke</a></i>. In an interview with <a href="/wiki/Digital_Spy" title="Digital Spy">Digital Spy</a>, Parke stated that it was really challenging to record "Because of You." He added, "I asked the producer if we could leave out some of the big notes. We left them until the end and I was actually a bit scared by the noise that came out of me - I didn't know I could sound that loud!"<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-133"><a href="#cite_note-133">[133]</a></sup> "Because of You" was also covered by Kim Bo Kyung, who was a contestant in South Korean singing competition show, <i><a href="/wiki/Superstar_K2" title="Superstar K2">Superstar K2</a>.</i> Her performance received positive response from the judges and was considered as one of the highlights in the show even though she failed to advance into the Top 11.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-134"><a href="#cite_note-134">[134]</a></sup> Following her elimination, she recorded the studio version of "Because of You" which was released as a digital download by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sony_Music_Entertainment" title="Sony Music Entertainment">Sony Music Entertainment</a> due to an overwhelming demand.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-135"><a href="#cite_note-135">[135]</a></sup> She also received a personal video message from Clarkson who gave her words of advice and support.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-136"><a href="#cite_note-136">[136]</a></sup> The song also was covered by <a href="/wiki/Orange_Caramel" title="Orange Caramel">Orange Caramel</a>, a South Korean <a href="/wiki/Girl_group" title="Girl group">girl group</a>, on Christmas Day for <a href="/wiki/Munhwa_Broadcasting_Corporation" title="Munhwa Broadcasting Corporation">MBC</a>'s special programme, "ICON".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-137"><a href="#cite_note-137">[137]</a></sup> Besides these cover versions, "Because of You" was also included in international soundtrack to Brazilian soap opera <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bel%C3%ADssima" title="Belíssima">Belíssima</a></i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-138"><a href="#cite_note-138">[138]</a></sup></p>

<p>In 2007, Clarkson re-recorded "Because of You" as a duet with American country singer <a href="/wiki/Reba_McEntire" title="Reba McEntire">Reba McEntire</a>. The song was released as a single on May 15, 2007, as the lead single for McEntire's album, <i><a href="/wiki/Reba:_Duets" title="Reba: Duets">Reba: Duets</a></i>. The duet garnered mixed reviews from critics who felt that even though McEntire's singing was pleasant, she brought nothing new to the song. At the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/50th_Grammy_Awards" title="50th Grammy Awards">50th Grammy Awards</a>, McEntire and Clarkson received a nomination for Best Vocal Country Collaboration for the song. In the United States, "Because of You" became McEntire's seventh song to peak at number two at <a href="/wiki/Hot_Country_Songs" title="Hot Country Songs">Hot Country Songs</a>. It also became Clarkson's first song to appear on the chart. The music video was directed by <a href="/wiki/Roman_White" title="Roman White">Roman White</a> which depicts McEntire and Clarkson as two retro Hollywood lounge singers. The plot centers on Clarkson's relationship with her abusive partner which is witnessed by McEntire. The song was performed live by the two singers in various venues, notably at the <a href="/wiki/Academy_of_Country_Music#2007" title="Academy of Country Music">42nd Annual Academy of Country Music Awards</a> and during their <a href="/wiki/2_Worlds_2_Voices_Tour" title="2 Worlds 2 Voices Tour">2 Worlds 2 Voices Tour</a>.</p>

<td class="mbox-text" colspan="2" style="line-height:1.1em"><span><i>Problems playing this file? See <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Media_help" title="Wikipedia:Media help">media help</a>.</i></span></td>
</tr>
</table>
<p>According to McEntire, Clarkson was the first singer to pair up with her for the album <i><a href="/wiki/Reba:_Duets" title="Reba: Duets">Reba: Duets</a></i> (2007).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pair_139-0"><a href="#cite_note-pair-139">[139]</a></sup> She also claimed that "Because of You" was not the original song to be included in the album; it was another song that she recorded with Clarkson, titled "A Lot Like You."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Scripps_Networks_Interactive_140-0"><a href="#cite_note-Scripps_Networks_Interactive-140">[140]</a></sup> McEntire explained that it was Narvel, her husband, who convinced her to go back in the studio and record "Because of You" after he heard both McEntire and Clarkson rehearsing the song.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pair_139-1"><a href="#cite_note-pair-139">[139]</a></sup> She expressed, "Narvel saw it. That wasn't one of the songs we had talked about recording – matter of fact, Kelly and I had already recorded a song, 'A Lot Like You,' for the duet project, and he said, 'You've got to do this one together,' so we did."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Scripps_Networks_Interactive_140-1"><a href="#cite_note-Scripps_Networks_Interactive-140">[140]</a></sup> Musically, the song is different from the original version. Thom Jhurek of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Allmusic" title="Allmusic">Allmusic</a> described the duet version as "a big, overblown power ballad" which incorporates "guitars compressed to the breaking point, sweeping strings, and enormous crashing cymbals."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-thom_141-0"><a href="#cite_note-thom-141">[141]</a></sup> The use of violin was also incorporated into the duet, giving it a melodramatic quality that was deemed "unnecessary" by Nancy Dunham of Blogcritics.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-blogcritics_142-0"><a href="#cite_note-blogcritics-142">[142]</a></sup> The song was officially sent to radio stations on May 15, 2007, as the lead single from the album.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-143"><a href="#cite_note-143">[143]</a></sup> It was added to country radio playlists on May 28, 2007.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-us_radio_144-0"><a href="#cite_note-us_radio-144">[144]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Critical_reception_2">Critical reception</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Because_of_You_(Kelly_Clarkson_song)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Critical reception">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The song received mixed reviews from critics. Lana Cooper of <a href="/wiki/PopMatters" title="PopMatters">PopMatters</a> loved the duet and deemed it as "the most unique track on the album."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-popmattersduo_145-0"><a href="#cite_note-popmattersduo-145">[145]</a></sup> She also felt that McEntire and Clarkson complemented each other in the song, writing "The double-feature cover of Clarkson’s hit showcases two women with exceptional and distinctive voices playing to one another’s strengths."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-popmattersduo_145-1"><a href="#cite_note-popmattersduo-145">[145]</a></sup> The same opinion was echoed by Nancy Dunham of Blogcritics who believed that "the two use just the right amount of vocal passion to make the ardent lyrics come alive, but stay out of the cheese zone."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-blogcritics_142-1"><a href="#cite_note-blogcritics-142">[142]</a></sup> Scott Sexton of <a href="/wiki/About.com" title="About.com">About.com</a> lauded the duet version of the song, writing "As of now anything Reba touches turns to gold, but with this hit alone she has a great shot at platinum."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-146"><a href="#cite_note-146">[146]</a></sup> Kevin John Coyne of Country Universe praised McEntire's beautiful singing although he said that she did not bring "anything new" to the song.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-countryuniverse_147-0"><a href="#cite_note-countryuniverse-147">[147]</a></sup> He also added that the song "had the potential to be reworked into an interesting mother/daughter confrontation" but he was disappointed because McEntire did not change the viewpoints of the song.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-countryuniverse_147-1"><a href="#cite_note-countryuniverse-147">[147]</a></sup> He graded the production of the song as "C-", writing "The end result is the song doesn’t make any sense, and is just confusing to listen to."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-148"><a href="#cite_note-148">[148]</a></sup> Thom Jurek of Allmusic criticized the instrumentation of the song, saying "This could have been a <a href="/wiki/Meat_Loaf" title="Meat Loaf">Meat Loaf</a> reject from <a href="/wiki/Bat_Out_of_Hell_II:_Back_into_Hell" title="Bat Out of Hell II: Back into Hell">Bat Out of Hell II</a>."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-thom_141-1"><a href="#cite_note-thom-141">[141]</a></sup> Gayle Thompson of The Boot ranked "Because of You" at number ten in her list of "Top 20 Reba McEntire songs."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-149"><a href="#cite_note-149">[149]</a></sup> She also included both McEntire and Clarkson at number six for their duet of "Because of You" in her list of "Cross Country: Top 10 Country-Pop Duets."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-150"><a href="#cite_note-150">[150]</a></sup> Gary Trust of <i>Billboard</i> listed the pair as one of the 10 all-female hit collaborations that have scaled <i>Billboard</i> charts in recent years.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-151"><a href="#cite_note-151">[151]</a></sup> On March 5, 2013, <i><a href="/wiki/Billboard_(magazine)" title="Billboard (magazine)">Billboard</a></i> ranked the song #71 in its list of Top 100 American Idol Hits of All Time.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-152"><a href="#cite_note-152">[152]</a></sup></p>
<p>At the <a href="/wiki/Academy_of_Country_Music#2007" title="Academy of Country Music">42nd Annual Academy of Country Music Awards</a>, McEntire and Clarkson received a nomination in the category of Musical Event of the Year for "Because of You," but lost to <a href="/wiki/Tracy_Lawrence" title="Tracy Lawrence">Tracy Lawrence</a> with <a href="/wiki/Kenny_Chesney" title="Kenny Chesney">Kenny Chesney</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tim_McGraw" title="Tim McGraw">Tim McGraw</a> for their collaboration in "<a href="/wiki/Find_Out_Who_Your_Friends_Are" title="Find Out Who Your Friends Are">Find Out Who Your Friends Are</a>" (2006).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-153"><a href="#cite_note-153">[153]</a></sup> At the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/50th_Grammy_Awards" title="50th Grammy Awards">50th Grammy Awards</a>, McEntire and Clarkson received a nomination in the category of Best Vocal Country Collaboration for the song, but lost to <a href="/wiki/Willie_Nelson" title="Willie Nelson">Willie Nelson</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ray_Price_(musician)" title="Ray Price (musician)">Ray Price</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-154"><a href="#cite_note-154">[154]</a></sup> The pair also received a nomination for the Vocal Event of the Year at the <a href="/wiki/Academy_of_Country_Music#2008" title="Academy of Country Music">2008 Academy of Country Music</a>, but lost to Tracy Lawrence with Kenny Chesney and Tim McGraw for their collaboration in "Find Out Who Your Friends Are".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-155"><a href="#cite_note-155">[155]</a></sup> At the 2008 ASCAP Country Music Awards, the song was honoured with the Most Performed Songs award.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-156"><a href="#cite_note-156">[156]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Commercial_performance_2">Commercial performance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Because_of_You_(Kelly_Clarkson_song)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Commercial performance">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Reba_McEntire_%26_Kelly_Clarkson_-_Encore.jpg"><img alt="Image of two blond women walking down a step of stairs on the stage. An image of guitarist is seen standing next to them. Behind them, a set of drum and a cello are seen." class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1024" data-file-width="768" height="227" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/Reba_McEntire_%26_Kelly_Clarkson_-_Encore.jpg/170px-Reba_McEntire_%26_Kelly_Clarkson_-_Encore.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/Reba_McEntire_%26_Kelly_Clarkson_-_Encore.jpg/255px-Reba_McEntire_%26_Kelly_Clarkson_-_Encore.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/Reba_McEntire_%26_Kelly_Clarkson_-_Encore.jpg/340px-Reba_McEntire_%26_Kelly_Clarkson_-_Encore.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Reba_McEntire_%26_Kelly_Clarkson_-_Encore.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
McEntire and Clarkson singing "Because of You" as part of the encore in <a href="/wiki/2_Worlds_2_Voices_Tour" title="2 Worlds 2 Voices Tour">2 Worlds 2 Voices Tour</a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>In the United States, "Because of You" debuted at number 42 on the <a href="/wiki/Hot_Country_Songs" title="Hot Country Songs">Hot Country Songs</a> on the week ending June 2, 2007.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-157"><a href="#cite_note-157">[157]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-158"><a href="#cite_note-158">[158]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-159"><a href="#cite_note-159">[159]</a></sup> On the week ending September 8, 2007, the song jumped to its new peak at number two and was held off the top spot by <a href="/wiki/Rodney_Atkins" title="Rodney Atkins">Rodney Atkins</a>' "<a href="/wiki/These_Are_My_People" title="These Are My People">These Are My People</a>" (2007).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-160"><a href="#cite_note-160">[160]</a></sup> It became McEntire's seventh song to peak at number two, and her first in over ten years.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-161"><a href="#cite_note-161">[161]</a></sup> Had the song jumped to number one, it would have been McEntire's 23rd number one song on the chart as well as the first remake of a pop song to top Hot Country Songs since <a href="/wiki/Mark_Chesnutt" title="Mark Chesnutt">Mark Chesnutt</a>'s cover of <a href="/wiki/Aerosmith" title="Aerosmith">Aerosmith</a>'s "<a href="/wiki/I_Don%27t_Want_to_Miss_a_Thing" title="I Don't Want to Miss a Thing">I Don't Want to Miss a Thing</a>" spent two weeks at number one in 1999.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-162"><a href="#cite_note-162">[162]</a></sup> "Because of You" also made an appearance on the <i>Billboard</i> Hot 100 at number 52,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-163"><a href="#cite_note-163">[163]</a></sup> and peaked at number 50.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-164"><a href="#cite_note-164">[164]</a></sup> In Canada, the song peaked at number 36 on the week ending July 21, 2007.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-165"><a href="#cite_note-165">[165]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Music_video_2">Music video</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Because_of_You_(Kelly_Clarkson_song)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Music video">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The music video, directed by <a href="/wiki/Roman_White" title="Roman White">Roman White</a>, debuted on June 21, 2007.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-166"><a href="#cite_note-166">[166]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-167"><a href="#cite_note-167">[167]</a></sup> It depicts McEntire and Clarkson as 1930's Hollywood lounge singers. In the video, McEntire encounters Clarkson attempting to conceal a bruise inflicted by the latter's abusive partner. When Clarkson's boyfriend is fighting with her, McEntire leaves the dressing room. While performing on stage, Clarkson witnesses her boyfriend played by Andrew M. Springer flirting with another woman. After the performance, she smashes a vase out of anger in the dressing room. Her boyfriend enters the room to take her out for the rest of the evening. Though apprehensive, Clarkson leaves on his arm before looking back uncertainly at McEntire, who uncomfortably fiddles with a hairbrush as she watches them leave. The music video hit number one on CMT's <a href="/wiki/Top_20_Countdown" title="Top 20 Countdown">Top 20 Countdown</a> on September 13, 2007.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-168"><a href="#cite_note-168">[168]</a></sup> At the <a href="/wiki/CMT_Music_Awards#2008" title="CMT Music Awards">2008 CMT Music Awards</a>, the music video received nominations for three awards. It received a nomination for the Video of the Year, but lost to <a href="/wiki/Taylor_Swift" title="Taylor Swift">Taylor Swift</a>'s "<a href="/wiki/Our_Song_(Taylor_Swift_song)" title="Our Song (Taylor Swift song)">Our Song</a>" (2007) and for the Collaborative Video of the Year, but lost to <a href="/wiki/Bon_Jovi" title="Bon Jovi">Bon Jovi</a> featuring <a href="/wiki/LeAnn_Rimes" title="LeAnn Rimes">LeAnn Rimes</a>, "<a href="/wiki/Till_We_Ain%27t_Strangers_Anymore" title="Till We Ain't Strangers Anymore">Till We Ain't Strangers Anymore</a>" (2007). Roman White, who directed the music video, received a nomination for the Video Director of the Year, but lost to <a href="/wiki/Michael_Salomon" title="Michael Salomon">Michael Salomon</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-169"><a href="#cite_note-169">[169]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Live_performances_2">Live performances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Because_of_You_(Kelly_Clarkson_song)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Live performances">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>McEntire and Clarkson first performed "Because of You" together at the 42nd Annual Academy of Country Music Awards in May 2007.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-170"><a href="#cite_note-170">[170]</a></sup> A month later, the pair performed the song in an episode of <a href="/wiki/CMT_Crossroads" title="CMT Crossroads">CMT Crossroads</a> at <a href="/wiki/Ryman_Auditorium" title="Ryman Auditorium">Ryman Auditorium</a> which debuted on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Country_Music_Television" title="Country Music Television">Country Music Television</a> on June 24, 2007.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-171"><a href="#cite_note-171">[171]</a></sup> On September 19, 2007, they appeared on <i><a href="/wiki/The_Oprah_Winfrey_Show" title="The Oprah Winfrey Show">The Oprah Winfrey Show</a></i> where they sang the song together.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-172"><a href="#cite_note-172">[172]</a></sup> "Because of You" was also performed as the encore of the <a href="/wiki/2_Worlds_2_Voices_Tour" title="2 Worlds 2 Voices Tour">2 Worlds 2 Voices Tour</a> (2008), a co-headlining concert tour by McEntire and Clarkson.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-173"><a href="#cite_note-173">[173]</a></sup></p>
